  362. I just wanted to share a tip with everyone so that you can use the product easier. I live in Florida, where it is very hot and humid. After a few bad pulls where the wax melted on my skin and never firmed up, making it almost impossible to pull off quickly, I found out that my skin was too hot! As blood rushes to the surface of your skin, it gets hotter and hotter. A good tip is to keep an ice cube in a cup next to you, ice your skin down before you put the wax on, then dry with a paper towel, THEN warm the strips and put them on your skin. That way, you have hot wax going on a cold surface and immediately firming up, grabbing the hairs, and pulling them out once you pull the strip!
